(** * Pushout of a Monic is Monic, Pullback of an Epi is Epi *)
(** Contents
- Pushout of a Monic is Monic
- Pushout of a Monic is Pullback
- Pullback of an Epi is Epi
- Pullback of an Epi is Pushout
 *)

(** ** Introduction
We show that in abelian categories pushout of a Monic is a Monic and pullback of an Epi is an Epi.
Also, in this case the pushout diagram (resp. pullback diagram) is a pullback diagram (resp. pushout
diagram).

More precisely, let f : x --> y and g : x --> z be morphisms in an abelian category. Consider the
following pushout diagram
                            x ----g----> z
                          f |        in2 |
                            y ---in1---> w
If f is a Monic, then in2 is a Monic, [AbelianPushoutMonic2]. If g is a Monic, then in1 is a Monic,
[AbelianPushoutMonic1]. In both of the cases the above diagram is a pullback diagram,
[AbelianPushoutMonicisPullback1], [AbelianPushoutMonicisPullback2].

Let f : x --> z and g : y --> z be morphisms in an abelian category. Consider the following pullback
diagram
                            w ---pr1---> x
                       pr2  |          f |
                            y ----g----> z
If f is an Epi, then pr2 is an Epi, [AbelianPushoutEpi2], and if g is an Epi, then pr1 is an Epi,
[AbelianPushoutEpi1]. In both of the cases the above diagram is a pushout diagram,
[AbelianPullbackEpiisPushout1], [AbelianPullbackEpiisPushout2].

 *)
Section pushout_monic_pullback_epi.

  Context {A : AbelianPreCat}.
  (* Let hs : has_homsets A := homset_property A. *)

  Local Opaque Abelian.Equalizer.
  Local Opaque Abelian.Coequalizer.
  Local Opaque to_BinDirectSums.
  Local Opaque to_binop to_inv.


  (** ** Pushout of a Monic is Monic *)

  
A: AbelianPreCat
x, y, z: A
f: Monic A x y
g: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
Po: Pushout f g
isMonic (PushoutIn2 Po)

  
A: AbelianPreCat
x, y, z: A
f: Monic A x y
g: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
Po: Pushout f g
isMonic (PushoutIn2 Po)

    
A: AbelianPreCat
x, y, z: A
f: Monic A x y
g: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
Po: Pushout f g
DS:= to_BinDirectSums (AbelianToAdditive A) y z: BinDirectSum y z
isMonic (PushoutIn2 Po)

    
A: AbelianPreCat
x, y, z: A
f: Monic A x y
g: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
Po: Pushout f g
DS:= to_BinDirectSums (AbelianToAdditive A) y z: BinDirectSum y z
Po':= Pushout_from_Coequalizer_BinCoproduct A y z x f g
  (BinDirectSum_BinCoproduct
     (AbelianToAdditive A) DS)
  (Coequalizer A (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
     (g · ι₂%abgrcat)): Pushout f g
isMonic (PushoutIn2 Po)

    (* Transform the statement to a statement about other pushout *)

     (g · ι₂%abgrcat)): Pushout f g
iso:= z_iso_from_Pushout_to_Pushout Po Po': Isos.z_iso Po Po'
isMonic (PushoutIn2 Po)

isMonic
  (PushoutIn2 Po
   · PushoutArrow Po Po' (PushoutIn1 Po')
       (PushoutIn2 Po') (PushoutSqrCommutes Po'))

isMonic (PushoutIn2 Po')

∏ (z0 : AbelianToAdditive A)
(g0 : AbelianToAdditive A ⟦ z0, z ⟧),
g0 · PushoutIn2 Po' =
ZeroArrow (Additive.to_Zero (AbelianToAdditive A)) z0
  Po'
→ g0 =
  ZeroArrow (Additive.to_Zero (AbelianToAdditive A))
    z0 z

f: Monic A x y
g: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
Po: Pushout f g
DS:= to_BinDirectSums (AbelianToAdditive A) y z: BinDirectSum y z
Po':= Pushout_from_Coequalizer_BinCoproduct A y z x f g
  (BinDirectSum_BinCoproduct
     (AbelianToAdditive A) DS)
  (Coequalizer A (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
     (g · ι₂%abgrcat)): Pushout f g
iso:= z_iso_from_Pushout_to_Pushout Po Po': Isos.z_iso Po Po'
CE:= Coequalizer A (f · ι₁%abgrcat) (g · ι₂%abgrcat): Coequalizers.Coequalizer (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
  (g · ι₂%abgrcat)
CK:= AdditiveCoequalizerToCokernel
  (AbelianToAdditive A) (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
  (g · ι₂%abgrcat) CE: Cokernel (Additive.to_Zero (AbelianToAdditive A))
  (to_binop x DS (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
     (to_inv (g · ι₂%abgrcat)))
M1:= isMonic_to_binop_BinDirectSum1'
  (AbelianToAdditive A) f g DS: isMonic
  (to_binop x DS (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
     (to_inv (g · ι₂%abgrcat)))
K:= MonicToKernel' A
  (make_Monic (AbelianToAdditive A)
     (to_binop x DS (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
        (to_inv (g · ι₂%abgrcat))) M1) CK: Kernel (to_Zero A) (CokernelArrow CK)
z0: AbelianToAdditive A
g0: AbelianToAdditive A ⟦ z0, z ⟧
H: g0 · ι₂%abgrcat
· CoequalizerArrow
    (Coequalizer A (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
       (g · ι₂%abgrcat)) =
ZeroArrow (to_Zero A) z0
  (Coequalizer A (f · ι₁%abgrcat) (g · ι₂%abgrcat))
φ:= KernelIn (to_Zero A) K z0 (g0 · ι₂%abgrcat) H: A ⟦ z0, K ⟧
KComm:= KernelCommutes (to_Zero A) K z0
  (g0 · ι₂%abgrcat) H: φ · KernelArrow K = g0 · ι₂%abgrcat
g0 =
ZeroArrow (Additive.to_Zero (AbelianToAdditive A)) z0
  z

    (* The result follows from KComm and the fact that φ = ZeroArrow *)

Po':= make_Pushout g f Po (PushoutIn2 Po)
  (PushoutIn1 Po) (! PushoutSqrCommutes Po)
  (is_symmetric_isPushout (PushoutSqrCommutes Po)
     (isPushout_Pushout Po)): Pushout g f
isMonic (PushoutIn1 Po)

    use (AbelianPushoutMonic2 g f Po').
  Qed.

A: AbelianPreCat
x, y, z: A
f: Monic A x y
g: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
Po: Pushout f g
DS:= to_BinDirectSums (AbelianToAdditive A) y z: BinDirectSum y z
Po':= Pushout_from_Coequalizer_BinCoproduct A y z x f g
  (BinDirectSum_BinCoproduct
     (AbelianToAdditive A) DS)
  (Coequalizer A (f · ι₁%abgrcat)
     (g · ι₂%abgrcat)): Pushout f g
i:= z_iso_from_Pushout_to_Pushout Po Po': Isos.z_iso Po Po'
K:= MonicToKernel f: Kernel (to_Zero A)
  (CokernelArrow (to_Cokernels A x y f))
CK:= Abelian.Cokernel f: Cokernel (to_Zero A) f
e: A
h: A ⟦ e, y ⟧
k: A ⟦ e, z ⟧
Hk: h · PushoutIn1 Po' = k · PushoutIn2 Po'
y0: A ⟦ e, x ⟧
X: y0 · f = h × y0 · g = k
y0 · KernelArrow K = h
 exact (dirprod_pr1 X).
  Qed.

        (to_inv (π₂%abgrcat · g))) E1) K: Cokernel (to_Zero A) (KernelArrow K)

  (Equalizer A (π₁%abgrcat · f) (π₂%abgrcat · g))

ZeroArrow (to_Zero A)
  (Equalizer A (π₁%abgrcat · f) (π₂%abgrcat · g))
  z0

  z0

A: AbelianPreCat

f: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: Epi A y z

  (is_symmetric_isPullback
     (PullbackSqrCommutes Pb)
     (isPullback_Pullback Pb)): Pullback g f
isEpi (PullbackPr1 Pb)

    use (AbelianPullbackEpi2 g f Pb').
  Qed.

A: AbelianPreCat
x, y, z: A
f: Epi A x z
g: A ⟦ y, z ⟧
Pb: Pullback f g
DS:= to_BinDirectSums (AbelianToAdditive A) x y: BinDirectSum x y
Pb':= Pullback_from_Equalizer_BinProduct A x y z f g
  (BinDirectSum_BinProduct (AbelianToAdditive A)
     DS)
  (Equalizer A (π₁%abgrcat · f) (π₂%abgrcat · g)): Pullback f g
i:= z_iso_from_Pullback_to_Pullback Pb' Pb: Isos.z_iso Pb' Pb
CK:= EpiToCokernel f: Cokernel (to_Zero A)
  (KernelArrow (to_Kernels A x z f))
K:= Abelian.Kernel f: Kernel (to_Zero A) f
e: A
h: A ⟦ x, e ⟧
k: A ⟦ y, e ⟧
Hk: PullbackPr1 Pb' · h = PullbackPr2 Pb' · k
y0: A ⟦ z, e ⟧
X: f · y0 = h × g · y0 = k
CokernelArrow CK · y0 = h
 exact (dirprod_pr1 X).
  Qed.

A: AbelianPreCat
x, y, z: A
f: A ⟦ x, z ⟧
g: Epi A y z

     (PullbackSqrCommutes Pb)
     (isPullback_Pullback Pb)): Pullback g f
isPushout (PullbackPr2 Pb) (PullbackPr1 Pb) g f
  (! PullbackSqrCommutes Pb)
 exact (AbelianPullbackEpiisPushout1 g f Pb').
